	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'c647d2a6586174c94c25de124b82f1f63d2db142') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c647d2a6586174c94c25de124b82f1f63d2db142') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd857c1f54bbad41b702e19165965c92890ebf77e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c647d2a6586174c94c25de124b82f1f63d2db142') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') != '9d51f07f7a7bc1a2848b97b9a3704299ed33dbde') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== '9d51f07f7a7bc1a2848b97b9a3704299ed33dbde') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== 'cc11de9d98d75ea392b5b243a7180920ef11a1d1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== '9d51f07f7a7bc1a2848b97b9a3704299ed33dbde') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
		}
	}
}

			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php') !== 'c203c4bb7307c571d49eb9992a9fab82caffd22a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 634\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 634') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
